<name>William Amerman< /name><Time>1620586562183</Time><rating>5</rating>< text>
Rushed here for emergency care for our dear dog Kiba who had collapsed, not breathing. We got him breathing again, got him here and they took him in immediately. They kept us updated very regularly, every 15-20 mins. Even though they did not expect him to make it, they continued keeping him going per our requests, until finally after about an hour and a half we made the decision, based on their excellent sharing of information and prognosis, to let our little guy go. It was expensive, but I felt the quality of care was outstanding, as well as the empathy expressed and the process of saying goodbye in the private area behind the clinic. They helped us through such a traumatic experience.<//text>

<Rating>5<//Rating><text>It has taken a long time to do this review because of my grief.  I had such a hard time getting over my Mickey.  However i feel it is necessary to say how wonderful this hospital is.  I have had to put pets down before but I have never been treated with such respect and dignity.  I originally came in for a second opinion, as my vet at the time said over the phone well just come in and I will put him down.  Those were her very words !  So I went to Silicon Valley for an opinion and the Dr. who saw Mickey said, we could spend about 4-7 thousand to try but , I really think you have done a good job keeping him alive for as long as you have, it may be time to say good bye.  How eloquently put!  My poor Frenchie was born with a small breathing tube and was on medication his whole life,  he almost made it to ten years old.  I knew that the Dr. was saying it was ok to let him go, and Mickey knew it was time.  We made arrangements to come back to
euthanize, and they took us into a special room and said take your time, when the time came , the Dr. explained everything she was going to do.  I had Mickey on my lap, she gave him the first shot and he kissed her good bye.  Even the Dr. was in tears at this point.  After everything was over. about 3 days later I received a wonderful card that the whole office signed.  I can't tell you how much that meant!!!!  Thank you from the bottom of my heart. < Text>
Our pets, we love them, right? It's the reason as to why all of you are willing to immediately go to an animal emergency care center when you learned that your pet's health is in danger. However, like many other things in life, you will find wretched scums who will try to exploit this innocent love. This place, is filled with these kind of people. I would've remained ignorant of this, if it weren't for the fact that I've experienced it firsthand for myself.

I have a cat, who swallowed a 1.5 inch needle. I wasn't certain he swallowed it at the time, so I immediately looked for an emergency care center, and ended up taking him here to get an x-ray. I paid $410 dollars out of my pocket, anxious to know the results. However, I ended up having to spend for an agonizing 2.5 hours, when they originally claimed that they could get it done in 30 minutes. When I asked why it took so long, they claimed that they were "busy," despite the fact that there were only two other patients.

The results came in, and it was confirmed: My cat did swallowed a needle. The worry on my face was obvious. One of the staff, seeing this, clearly wanted to exploit this, for he said that to get the needle removed "right now," it would cost more than $9000. Right after he said that, he shrugged, and gave another offer, which is to pay $5500 to get it removed tomorrow morning. If it weren't for the fact that a family member earlier told me that an emergency surgery would've costed approximately $1000 - $2000, I've fallen for this trap. The person showed no compassion as I got my cat back, needle still in his stomach. Before leaving, I asked for a copy of the x-ray image.  They said they will email it to me by 6AM next morning, but I've never received it.  I left the building, and looked back, only to see that same person laughing with the others. I knew then, that I absolutely cannot trust this place.

As I got home, I instantaneously looked for another location. That same day, I found a local vet in Evergreen, with a very straightforward doctor who offered that we pay $1500 for x-ray, needle removal, AND medicine, all in one package. I immediately took his offer, and now, my cat is jumping about once again, a needle gone from his stomach.

But, it wasn't over yet. Believe or not, this scam disguised as a hospital called me a week later in an attempt to milk even more money out of me, oblivious to the fact that my cat already made the recovery. It wouldn't take a genius to know that I hung up at the spot.<//Text>

< Review>
Last year we had to get a jacket, gloves and beanie for my son who was headed up to the mountains for 6th grade science camp in March. Trying to find ski equipment late in the season was turning out to be both difficult and expensive. I remembered my friend telling me about this place so I did a search on Google and was able to locate them. I was able to purchase all the items for a little under $120. Unfortunately the jacket was a little too small so I had to return it for a larger one. This the salesgirl did with no problem (I had my receipt).

If you are looking for ski or snowboard apparel this is the first place you should start! They also carry a nice selection of snowboards and snowboard packages.< /Review>

<gmap_id>0x80dbfd7b5e442bb7:0x2db1822d24ffd7c4<//gmap_id>< Text>
Just finished my first Fox's Pizza Den pizza and IMHO was THE best pizza I've ever had.  The bread sticks were also great.  The gentleman who took my order was friendly and cheerful. I picked up myself and the lady who cashed me out was also friendly and cheerful.  The "Den" is a small little place and from what I observed was very clean. Pretty much your idealistic little pizza place.  They had patio tables outside their entrance door if you want to eat outside.  The price was very reasonable.  I got their Thursday special which was a large 2 topping pizza for $11.99 and I decided to get a side of their bread sticks.  I choose what the caller suggested which he said was his favorite.  In total a delicious pizza dinner with bread sticks for just shy of $17.  I will definitely be back.  Good job guys and gal :)< /Text>

<Date>1389971441968</Date><Rating>2< /Rating><Review>Meh.

Any park that is mainly concrete or pavement is not a park; it's a re-purposed parking lot.

Though the developers who helped create this park claim it is mainly for children, it is not child friendly. There's a small corner of the park with "toddler playground" equipment, but it is not grassed in, the creator or designer chose to use a cushy foam instead. The play equipment is actually pretty good, too bad the designers decided to make the rest of the park look like an outdoor conference room.

Though the intent was to have an area adults and children could play in and around, dogs outnumber children 20:1. The grassy knoll adjacent to the playground is fenced off indefinitely. It looks nice, but it fails in its original intent, fails in its most useful purpose (a dog park) and fails as any sort of park. There aren't even any decent shade trees and it is certainly not restful.

If taxpayer dollars helped create this area the public was bilked.</Review><Pics>None</Pics>< response>

<rating>4< /rating><Text>It's an old fashioned coffee shop/family diner style restaurant-the specials are great and the food overall is homey and tasty-great onion rings-order your fries extra crispy and you'll get hot fresh fries that are delicious-german pot roast, Turkey dinner on Sundays, California club sandwich-great omlettes that are hearty and full of goodies-real mashed potatos and a great collection of large meal sized salads-the service is friendly and once you start going they will know and remember you-they have worked hard from ten years ago when this place was just OK till now when it has been cleaned up and streamlined-it's a style of local, neighborhood food that is disappearing-I only held back one star because sometimes I think with a push they could kick it up a notch-potato salad isn't hard to make but they buy theirs-if they added a good pastry checf and did in house pies and turnovers it would make this a great location instead of just good-prices have moved up a bit but what hasn't and the quality is there-let';s keep Huff's around not to be confused with Hof's another local chain which is slowly disappearing<//Text><pics>None</pics>< Resp>

< text>
Whew!  I'm a huffin, I'm a puffin & now I'm ready for a nap!

BOGO entr√©e with purchase of 2 beverages

"Mel's Diner", aka Huff's, is an old-timey Americana diner, serving up bottomless cups of Joe & tummy-stuffing breakfast all day.  I haven't been here in over a decade, and the coupon was the perfect enticement to bring me back for a hot meal on a cool, windy November day.

Want cream in your coffee?  Then tilt back one of these cute little tins
(see pic)

Huff's has daily specials, with Wednesday's specials being peppercorn steak & AYCE BBQ ribs, respectively.  Unfortunately, we were told they were out.  Shucks!  I so was gonna go for the peppercorn steak.

Calling an audible, I went with the Avocado Breeze omelet-
Avocado, crispy bacon, tomatoes, sweet onions, cheddar & Jack cheese with a dollop of sour cream on top, the dish came with my choice of Western-style potatoes (with onions & bell peppers) & buttermilk biscuit

The hulking behemoth was stick to your ribs, comfort food.  The rich avocado slices enhanced by the crispy, salty bacon.  The potatoes were fork tender, with everything enhanced by a liberal dousing of Tabasco sauce.  Not crumbly, the biscuit was actually soft, which made it not as messy to eat.  Filling, hearty & under $10.  Not too shabby, Huff's.

Other food items include pancakes, bacon & eggs, pasta, pizza, burgers, sandwiches etc.  As previously mentioned, Huff's has daily specials to choose from.  For those looking for a cold one, beers are on tap including Shock Top.

Service was good.  We were told we could sit anywhere we like.  The staff regularly checked on us, making sure everything was to our liking.  Plenty of seating, with counter, booths & tables located around the premises.  We sat in the more private area on the left of the main entrance.  2 flatscreen TV's allowed us to watch Rachel Ray as we ate.  The cool thing about the chairs?  They've got wheels!  Genius!  No scuffing noises from moving chairs.  I acted as a little kid and rolled my way to & fro.  Now if only hoity toity places like Crustacean & Mastro's adopted wheeled seating.  That would be awesome! ;p

Parking is in a private lot at the El Dorado Center.  TJ Maxx is the anchor store, with Huff's being directly in front of the Dollar Tree.

Huff's is a step back in time, and it shows in the d√©cor.  However, it's homey & the food meets diner expectations.  The service was helpful & friendly, and considering I have 2 more BOGO coupons, it's a given I'll be coming back.

Recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM<//text>

I am very pleased with the services from NuggMD, for several reasons. 1) It is very easy to complete the approval process. 2) In case of rejection, the payment is reimbursed. 3) Very competitive prices, compared to other online providers for California as of today. 4) The doctor called me shortly after I completed the application.
